--- Row 17 ---
  : ALGORITHM GUIDE

--- Row 18 ---
  : Etsy Search Algorithm:

--- Row 19 ---
  : - Recency boost: new listings get 24-48hr visibility boost. Relist every 2-3 days.

--- Row 20 ---
  : - Relevancy: first 3 words of title are most weighted. Put exact search term first.

--- Row 21 ---
  : - Quality score: conversion rate + favorites + shop reviews matter.

--- Row 22 ---
  : - Tags: use all 13. Long-tail > generic ("minimalist gold necklace" > "jewelry").

--- Row 23 ---
  : - Free shipping: Etsy penalizes listings without free shipping. Bake into price.

--- Row 24 ---

--- Row 25 ---
  : eBay Best Match:

--- Row 26 ---
  : - Recent sales velocity matters most. Price competitively on first 5 sales.

--- Row 27 ---
  : - Item specifics: fill EVERY field. eBay penalizes incomplete listings.

--- Row 28 ---
  : - Promoted listings: 2-5% ad rate to boost visibility initially.

--- Row 29 ---
  : SHADOWBAN AVOIDANCE

--- Row 30 ---
  : Etsy: Never copy-paste descriptions from other listings (duplicate content flag). Never use same photos as another seller. Never list >50 items in 24hr (new shop). Ramp: 5/day week 1, 10/day week 2, 20/day week 3.

--- Row 31 ---
  : eBay: Below Standard = death. Ship within stated handling time. Never cancel orders. Keep defect rate <2%.

--- Row 32 ---
  : LLM-IN-THE-LOOP

--- Row 33 ---
  : Claude runs on 6hr cron: scrape → analyze → score → list → monitor sales → delist losers → find replacements. Fully autonomous after initial shop setup.

--- Row 34 ---
  : MANUAL FIRST

--- Row 35 ---
  : Week 1-2: Manually list 10 products. Validate demand. Test margins. Learn platform rules.

--- Row 36 ---
  : AUTOMATE AFTER

--- Row 37 ---
  : Week 3+: Playwright + Claude API + Etsy API. Full loop. Human only handles customer service escalations.

--- Row 117 ---
  : ALGORITHM GUIDE

--- Row 118 ---
  : YouTube Algorithm Deep Dive:

--- Row 119 ---
  : - CTR (Click-Through Rate): #1 factor. Must be >5%. Thumbnail + title = 80% of success.

--- Row 120 ---
  : - AVD (Average View Duration): must be >50% of video length. Front-load value. Open loops.

--- Row 121 ---
  : - First 48 hours: YouTube tests with small audience. High CTR + AVD = wider distribution.

--- Row 122 ---
  : - Session time: videos that keep people on YouTube get boosted. End screens + playlists.

--- Row 123 ---
  : - Upload consistency: same time, same days. YouTube learns your schedule.

--- Row 124 ---
  : - Shorts vs Longform: separate algorithms. Shorts viewers rarely convert to longform. Run separately.

--- Row 125 ---
  : - Community tab: post polls/updates. Engagement signals activity.

--- Row 126 ---
  : - Revenue niches by CPM: Finance ($15-30), Tech ($12-25), Business ($10-20), Health ($8-15), Gaming ($2-5).

--- Row 127 ---
  : SHADOWBAN AVOIDANCE

--- Row 128 ---
  : YouTube:

--- Row 129 ---
  : - Community Guidelines strikes: 3 strikes in 90 days = termination. Avoid controversial topics.

--- Row 130 ---
  : - Reused content: YouTube detects recycled footage. Use >50% original or heavily edited content.

--- Row 131 ---
  : - AI disclosure: YouTube requires AI content labeling since March 2024. Always check the "altered/synthetic" box.

--- Row 132 ---
  : - Music copyright: use royalty-free only (Epidemic Sound, Artlist, or YouTube Audio Library).

--- Row 133 ---
  : - Title/thumbnail mismatch: clickbait without delivery = low AVD = algorithm punishment.

--- Row 134 ---
  : - Comment engagement: reply to first 10 comments within 1 hour. Signals active creator.

--- Row 135 ---
  : LLM-IN-THE-LOOP

--- Row 136 ---
  : Daily: Claude writes 1 script → ElevenLabs voices → Kling generates visuals → CapCut assembles → YouTube API uploads → Claude analyzes last 7 days performance → adjusts topics/hooks.

  : MANUAL FIRST

--- Row 138 ---
  : Week 1-2: Make 3 videos manually. Learn what CTR/AVD looks like. Study top channels in niche.

--- Row 139 ---
  : AUTOMATE AFTER

--- Row 140 ---
  : Week 3+: Full pipeline. Human does final quality check on thumbnail + first 30 seconds only.

--- Row 45 ---
  : THE PRINTMAXX THESIS

--- Row 46 ---
  : We are in a 12-36 month window where LLM-in-the-loop automation creates structural alpha across ecommerce, content, outbound, apps, and finance.

--- Row 47 ---
  : The alpha exists because: (1) most people dont know how to build LLM automation pipelines, (2) those who do are focused on building tools, not using them to print, (3) the tools are free or near-free.

--- Row 48 ---
  : The edge narrows as: (1) no-code LLM tools mature (make.com, n8n templates), (2) platform detection improves, (3) competition increases in each vertical.

--- Row 49 ---
  : Strategy: run ALL 37 ops simultaneously. Each op is a lottery ticket. The portfolio approach guarantees at least 3-5 winners. Winners get doubled down.

--- Row 50 ---
  : Manual first → validate unit economics → automate → scale. Never automate before validating. Never scale before automating.

--- Row 51 ---
  : The compounding effect: social accounts promote newsletters which promote apps which fund ads which amplify everything. Every op feeds every other op.
